28.16(1): sngags kyi mthu stobs kyis rngams gsas kyi sku ru grol/ 'dod chags gnas 'gyur 
28.17(1): ba'i 'brug chen sbyin pa chen po'i rang bzhin du gyur pas/ lha bye brag dngos med

28.19(1): mthus dbal gsas kyi sku ru grol/ phrag dog gnas 'gyur ba'i khyung chen yangs pa 
28.20(1): chen po'i rang bzhin du gsal/ lha dga' ba don grub kyi sku ru grol/ byin rlabs 
28.21(1): stobs kyis bya ba nan tan gyi ye shes su shar/ sngags kyi mthus gtum gsas kyi sku ru 
29.1(1): grol/ de yang nyon mongs pa lngar shar bas/ de las 'phags na sku lngar gsal zhes 
29.2(1): bya'o/ /gdan la 'phags pa'i sa bon lha ru sprul/ bsnyen pa'i bskur btab gzhung 
29.3(1): ltar lha yang bskyed/ de yang bskyed pa'i lha des gdan de byin gyis brlab/ don du

29.5(1): 'dom gru mtho tshon ye shes stobs kyi khyad/ mnyam nyid ye shes thob na gdan la mtho

29.8(1): rang 'gyur gdan gyi 'gyur tshul gyi le'u ste bcu pa'o/ //
29.9(1): 7 yang gsungs pa spyan drangs bzhugs su gsol ba/ dbyings nas spyan drangs

29.21(1): pa la bskyed pa ni nang gi gzhal yas su bzhugs/ gtor ma la bskyed pa'i gsang 
30.1(1): ba'i gzhal yas su bzhugs/ / rang lus la bskyed pa yang gsang gi gzhal yas su 
30.2(1): bzhugs/ ji ltar bzhugs na/ dkyil 'khor la bye ma la mar thim pa ltar bzhugs/

30.5(1): bzhugs/ don dam pa dkyil 'khor la bskyed dbang gi tshul du bzhugs/ bum pa

104.2(1): gshen lha 'od dkar gzigs so zhus pas/ skyes pa des 'di skad gsungs so/ /yong 
104.3(1): snang srid spangs pa'i pha rol na/ nam mkha' rgya mtsho ngas ma mthong / nam mkha' 
104.4(1): spangs pa'i pha rol na/ gshen lha 'dug pa ngas ma mthong / thegs rgyud spangs pa'i

104.6(1): gshen lha 'dug pa ngas ma mthong / zhes gsungs so/ /

104.8(1): bzhugs na/ snang srid phyi nang dang lus mgo bzhug tu 'jig rten mtha' dbus su 
104.9(1): rtsal na rnyed dam rnyed par 'gyur ram/ zhes gsungs so/ /'o rigs kyi bu ston pa

104.11(1): ro/ /snang srid 'di spangs pa'i pha rol gzhan nas kyang snyed par mi 'gyur ro/ /lus 
104.12(1): mgo mjug tu rtsal yang snyed par mi 'gyur ro/ /lus spang pa'i pha rol gzhan nas 
104.13(1): kyang snyed par mi 'gyur ro/ /mtha' dang dbus spangs pa'i pha rol nas kyang snyed 
104.14(1): par mi 'gyur ro/ /yang gsol ba skyes bu chen po khyod yul gang na gnas/ rta ni ci 
104.15(1): rigs/ mi ni ci'i cho/ da ni gar gshegs/ gshen lha 'od dkar gyi khungs shig khyod 
104.16(1): la cis kyang mnga' bas bstan pa zhu/ zhes gsol bas/ 'o skyes bu dad pa dang ldan 
104.17(1): pa/ bdag gi yul ni dbyings kyi yul/ bdag gi rta ni yid kyi rta/ bdag ni rig pa 
104.18(1): sems kyi mi/ nga 'ongs sa ni dbyings nas 'ongs/ 'gro ba ni klong du 'gro/ bzhugs 
104.19(1): pa ni ye shes chen po'i ngang na bzhugs/ khyod kyis ma bgrod na gshen lha'i yul du

105.11(1): bu cig gis bar bcad/ nges pa'i don ni gang bslab par bgyi ba lags/ ston

107.1(1): 7 gsas mkhar rin po che spyi spungs zhes bya ba ni/ bon gyi sgo mo brgyad khri bzhi

296.21(1): chen 'gas gcig rjes gnyis 'jug gis bsam bzhin du brda chad khag log 'grel 
296.22(1): byas te rjes 'dzin rnams mgo rmongs su bcug pa mthong / 'di dag ni rgyal khab dang mi 
297.1(1): rigs/  chos lugs bcas gang la yang mthun sgril dang bde skyid kyi bkag rdo ru 'gyur 
297.2(1): gshis/ 'dir bon gyi gzhung lugs ngo ma shes 'dod na bon gyi gsung rab dpe cha 'di 
297.3(1): lta bu la blta klog dang zhib 'jug gnang re'i ched dang / g.yung drung bon gyi bla sprul 
297.4(1): mkhas dbang mang pos yun ring re bskul byas pa'i rkyen dang / rgya che'i bod yig klog 
297.5(1): pa po yongs la blta bde 'khyer sla'i cha rkyen du dmigs nas/ ston pa'i gsung rab lung 
297.6(1): gi bon rin po che'i skor deb phreng brgya dang lnga bcu can zhig yig dkar gyi lam nas 
297.7(1): legs bsgrigs byas te/ rje smra seng bla ma'i gsung gi byin rlabs las 'phos pa/ g.yung 
297.8(1): drung bon gyi rgyud gzhung rin po che'i khrod kyi thun mong min pa'i brda chad/[ <<]gsung rab 
297.9(1): sgo mdzod Rin po che'i glegs bam[>>]zhes pa dpe tshogs spyi chings kyi mtshan du gsol nas 
297.10(1): dpar 'grems zhus pa yin/
297.11(1): zhus dag thad las rim dngos la thog ma'i ma dpe gang la byas pa/ bar du dpe cha 
297.12(1): gang du bsdur ba/ bsdur ba'i legs cha gang zhig thon pa sogs glegs bam so so'i nang 
297.13(1): dang mjug gi zhus bsgrigs gsal bshad du bris yod/ mdor na nged las mi yongs 
297.14(1): kyis spyi lo 2011lo nas bzung mi lo lnga yi ring dad pa dag snang dang rang gi dge sbyor 
297.15(1): dang bstan la zhabs phyi gtso bzung thog deb rer tshar grangs bco lnga nas nyi shu bar 
297.16(1): zhus dag byas yod pas sngar las lhag pa'i legs cha zhig thon yod pa'i re ba yod/ 'on 
297.17(1): kyang re 'ga' ma dpe gcig ma gtogs bsdur ya ma rnyed pa dang / re 'ga' bsdur ya 
297.18(1): du ma rnyed kyang bris pa'i chad lhag sogs kyis gcig mtshungs med pa dang / nged zhus 
297.19(1): sgrig pa tsho'i mkhyen dpyod tshad brgal can min pa bcas dang rjes 'gro byas pas nor 
297.20(1): 'khrul gyis bslad pa'ang yod nges pas/ rjes gzigs mkhan rnam pas su dang gang la 
297.21(1): khag dkri med pa rang bstan rang skyong gi 'gan 'khri gtsang ma phrag tu khur ste bstan pa 
297.22(1): rin po che'i ched du nor 'khrul yo bsrang dag ther gnang ba'i skul ma zhu rgyu dang /
298.1(1): mthar don du nged [<<]g.yung drung bon gyi bka' brten dpe rnying phyogs bsgrigs khang [>>]
298.2(1): gis las don rlabs chen 'di 'dra zhig legs grub byung ba ni/ rig gzhung 'di dang 
298.3(1): bstan pa 'di la lhag bsam can gyis phyar gru mnyam 'degs byas pa las byung ba 
298.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa 
298.5(1): rnam gnyis nas thugs khur rgyab skyor tshad med gnang ba dang / lhag par du dus rab 
298.6(1): kyi gnyan 'phrang mang po'i nang tshe srog 'ben dang bsdos te srung skyong byas pa'i dpe cha 
298.7(1): g.yar ba'i dpe bdag rnam pa dang / de bzhin nga tsho'i bstan don gyi bya ba kun la 
298.8(1): mthun sbyor gnang ba ma tshad dpe tshogs 'di dpar skrun skabs su yang ma bskul dang 
298.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
298.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas 
298.11(1): thugs rje che zhu rgyu dang / gsung rab dag bzhengs byas pa'i dge ba'i tshogs 'dis/
298.12(1): 7 skyabs rje rgyal ba sman ri ba'i mkhan slob rnam gnyis gtsos ris su ma chad pa'i 
298.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
298.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
298.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
298.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
298.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
298.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
298.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi
